In order of completion. Gonna read my favorite poems from each before i return to NYC tonight. Carry them with me. I like to read poetry when i travel, keep them in my pocket.\nListed: \n@anaffy's #BlackGirlMansion I took to Memphis Civil Rights spring break trip.\n.\n.\n.\n@nayyirah.waheed's #salt &amp; @lyrispect's #ThePrecursor with me in London.\n.\n.\n.\nfirst &amp; foremost Poetry and otherwise life Mother, @yolandawisher's #MonkEatsAfro I took to Ghana but finished in Philly.\n.\n.\n.\n#MajorJackson's #LeavingSaturn, the first collection I ever got, I finished in Philly.\n.\n.\n.\n@jj_bola's #WORD + @lutherxhughes' #M i read mostly in Allentown &amp; to grad school visits.\n.\n.\n.\nand @nifmuhammad's #TheCrownAintWorthMuch accompanied me on these New York streets.\n.\n.\n.\nWill be finishing #trigger by my sister bae @venusselenite, first Black trans woman out of out Lousianna to publish a book of poetry, mad soon. (not pictured. It's in NYC :( )\n.\n.\n.\nI find myself digging back through their works today. To find peace. To truly come home. To find a pillow, a shoulder. To remember. To step out fresh and be on some new shit. Please support Black poets. Please support Black artists (especially if they be Trans, Queer, Woman). We do a lot for y'all -- at least, it's fact these people here, and more, have done a lot for me... Love y'all. When I release my debut collection, you already know who's going in the acknowledgements ;) 💜✨\n#blackcreatives #goodwritersreadgood #WriteOnBeFree #blackartists #poetry #poems #poet #blackqueermagic class=\"yopto-main yotpo-regular-box  yotpo-loc\"> Reading @neilicorn in the Philadelphia airport\nand I've located\nan outlet\nbut no\nBuddhist monks. It is raining\nthe news speaks of Syria\nas I eat waffle fries.\nDo you know how loud\nthe souls of your shoes sound\non airport terminal tiles?\nThose around me are lost,\ndirectly in front of me there are\nthree laptops,\nI see two men,\nboth losing hair,\ncircling newspapers and I refuse to count the phones.\n.\n.\n.\n.\n.\n.\n.\n.\n<span lei lo adorava. Adorava il fatto che dovevo baciarla sedici volte o ventiquattro volte prima che lei andasse via se era Mercoledì.\nE adesso, non riesco a respirare perché penso che lui la bacia solo una volta. E non gli importa se quel bacio è perfetto o no.\nLa rivoglio così tanto che LASCIO LA PORTA APERTA E LE LUCI ACCESE. \"Disturbo Ossessivo Compulsivo\" Neil Hilborn\n\n<span <div class=\"yotpo-header-element\"> <label class=\"yotpo-user-name pull-left yotpo-instagram-username\"> vernonjordaniii </label> <br> <label class=\"yotpo-instagram-location\"> Germantown </label> </div> <div class=\"yotpo-header-element yotpo-header-actions\"> <label class=\"y-label yotpo-review-date\"> 01/26/17 </label> </div> </div> <div class=\"yopto-main yotpo-regular-box  yotpo-loc\"> all the poetry collections ive finished reading since 2013. In order of completion. Gonna read my favorite poems from each before i return to NYC tonight. Carry them with me. I like to read poetry when i travel, keep them in my pocket.\nListed: \n@anaffy's #BlackGirlMansion I took to Memphis Civil Rights spring break trip.\n.\n.\n.\n@nayyirah.waheed's <span class=\"yotpo-instagram-hashtag\">#salt</span> &amp; @lyrispect's #ThePrecursor with me in London.\n.\n.\n.\nfirst &amp; foremost Poetry and otherwise life Mother, @yolandawisher's #MonkEatsAfro I took to Ghana but finished in Philly.\n.\n.\n.\n#MajorJackson's #LeavingSaturn, the first collection I ever got, I finished in Philly.\n.\n.\n.\n@jj_bola's #WORD + @lutherxhughes' #M i read mostly in Allentown &amp; to grad school visits.\n.\n.\n.\nand @nifmuhammad's #TheCrownAintWorthMuch accompanied me on these New York streets.\n.\n.\n.\nWill be finishing <span class=\"yotpo-instagram-hashtag\">#trigger</span> by my sister bae @venusselenite, first Black trans woman out of out Lousianna to publish a book of poetry, mad soon. (not pictured. It's in NYC :( )\n.\n.\n.\nI find myself digging back through their works today. To find peace. To truly come home. To find a pillow, a shoulder. To remember. To step out fresh and be on some new shit. Please support Black poets. Please support Black artists (especially if they be Trans, Queer, Woman). We do a lot for y'all -- at least, it's fact these people here, and more, have done a lot for me... Love y'all. When I release my debut collection, you already know who's going in the acknowledgements ;) <img draggable=\"false\" class=\"emoji\" alt=\"💜\" subcompact that just could not wait to meet you; maybe things do happen for a reason but that reason is stupid. Maybe your brother fell out of a window only because he's an asshole. I love you, but I can't keep letting you show up where I am and remind me of what I said to you all those times I was drunk that one time. Most of them were just hurtful nonsense, but I am proud of \"You are like a comet: every so often you come around to fuck up my shit.\" \" #PoemsByNeilHilborn #OurNumberedDays #ButtonPoetry </div>
